  19 #include <stdint.h>

  21 /* The conversion table to UCS4 has almost no holes.  It can be generated with:
  22 
  23    egrep '^0x' /mnt/cdrom/unix/mappings/eastasia/gb/gb2312.txt |
  24    perl tab.pl
  25 
  26    where tab.pl is:
  27    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  28    $n=0;
  29    while (<>) {
  30      local($gb, $ucs4, %rest) = split;
  31      local($u)=hex($ucs4);
  32      local($g)=hex($gb);
  33      printf ("\n ") if ($n % 4 eq 0);
  34      ++$n;
  35      printf (" [0x%04x] = 0x%04x,",
  36              int(($g - 0x2121) / 256) * 94 + (($g - 0x2121) & 0xff), $u);
  37    }
  38    printf ("\n");
  39    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  40  */
